Location:
This is your strength, how hard you can deliver a blow, how much force you can use, and how ripping your muscles are! Each level of strength requires 1 AP.
This is your endurance, this is how long you can run, how far you can push yourself, how many hits you can take! Each level of endurance requires 1 AP.
This is your agilty, this is how fast you can move, how easily you can dodge, how quick you can swing your axe! Each level of agilty requires 1 AP.
This is your luck, your chance to find good fortune, your chance for your blade to find your enemies weakness, your chance for the universe to give you a break! Each level of luck requires 5 AP.
